<text>We stopped here for dinner on our drive from San Diego to a pumpkin patch in Chino Hills. All I'll say is dont judge the quality of food based on the shop's appearance from the outside. It was delicious!!!

The gentleman working, I'm assuming the owner, set up table and chairs outside the restaurant to stay within the county's COVID-19 restriction. The inside of the shop was immaculately clean from what I could see through the windows. The gentleman was an attentive and gracious host, waiter, AND chef! The food took a bit of time but that's to be expected when it's literally one person running the enture shop!

I grew up in Little Saigon in OC, so I know good pho. His is phenomenal!!! I got the rare beef pho, my teen got the beef banh mi, my 10yo got the chicken and rice plate, and my partner got the shrimp pad Thai and shrimp spring rolls. Everything was light years beyond our already high expectations. Our friends, who recently spent 2 weeks in VN for a wedding, also could not stop talking about how good the food was.

tl;dr - Excellent food worthy of the high ratings on both Yelp and Google. Worth the short trip off nearby freeways whether you're local or passing through.< /text><UserId.>110696760264332775636< /UserId.><Response>None</Response><user_name>Deborah Gardner< /user_name><Pics>None<//Pics></record></dataset><record>

< text>
The location and management are amazing. (AT THE CREEK) I've read different post about bad reviews and it must not be from the Creek managers. There are different sections here at the Homestead and I live in the Creek. Moved in in December of this year and had a few issues that have all been resolved since then.

PROBLEMS:
-Neighbors on hard drugs trash diving, yelling and waking me and my wife up 4-5 times every week. (Problem solved. They have been given multiple friendly warnings by management and myself and decided to cause more issues and since then are now all evicted.)
-Security not bening seen around the property at night. (There are still nights where security is not seen or that guard that doesn't do their job but some of them are seen on a regular and friendly. Would be nice to have the company send better guards or choose a different company)

POSITIVES:
-Alyssa and Christy have been extremely supportive throughout all complains and concerns. Even giving updates on more serious concerns
-Hot water was out at 7am and back up and running by 10am
-Road repairs have happened since we have been here
-Tree removal and trimming has happened in our short stay. (Much needed in some areas)
-Pool Spa was down for only 4 days after I informed them it was not working
-Have had a building inspection to test fire/smoke and CO2 alarms
-Set up insect and bug removal in areas needed and upon request.
-Water bill is cheaper then our last 2 apartments even though it's evenly distributed between all tenants
-Pool and BBQ areas always clean and presentable.
-Friendly neighbors
-No matte what time or day I can always find a washer and dryer available in the laundry room.

WHAT I WOULD RECOMMEND:

-More trash bins in the trash enclosures. Holidays and summer the bins get overfilled at times. Maintenance comes by and clean the area and puts things in the trash people miss but it would be nice to have more bins for the trash
-Being more strict with parking rules. Two vehicle passes should be permitted to each renter and only cars with a pass should be allowed to park behind the gates. Allowing only tenants to utilize closer parking spots. Also marking and removing vehicles permanently parked in open spots or parked for longer than a week in one spot. This isn't a storage garage and shouldn't be allowed to be treated as such.

Easily said that this is a great, friendly and we'll managed area. My experience has been great since I've moved in and I can't wait to see what more they do throughout the year.</text>

< text>
Though the pizza here was as tasty as any other Round Table I've eaten at, I find that, for what we had it was overpriced - please read on and you'll see why. Let me preface this with the fact we had just come from settling my elderly father in after having had surgery so we were mentally exhausted. We asked for specials and were told there was only one for a discount on an extra large pizza. There being just two of us that wouldn't work. We ordered a medium pepperoni for $18.00 only to see a window sticker as we sat down for a large pepperoni for $16.00!  What gives?!?!  We asked for the specials and the person clearly knew what type of pizza we wanted so why not tell us about this deal?  A few extra slices to bring home is worth paying less for the next size up.  One last complaint - when I asked for a box for our leftover pizza I was sent clear to the back of the store to pick up my own box. I've NEVER had to do that anywhere else and it felt very unsavory.  It will be a very long time before I go here again simply for the fact their customer service, in my opinion, was non-existent.< /text>

< Rating>
1</Rating>
<Review>3/10/15

I've been coming to this RT since my sister and I were little kids. We used to play on the Simpsons arcade machine at the front of the place before they remodeled it years ago. When my sister died unexpectedly a couple of weeks ago, my co-workers helped out my family by bringing homemade dinner to my parents and family every night of the week. The night before the funeral they ordered a Large and X-Large pizza for delivery to my parent's home, a mile away from this location. A special request to make heart-shaped pizza was included on the online order, and the pizzas were customized to end up with one meat and one veggie.

I received a call around 5 pm from RT - I had nothing to do with the ordering, as I'd been with my family all day handling funeral prep. They let me know that they weren't currently making the heart-shaped pizzas, and that pizza would arrive in about 40 minutes. However, it had been requested by the office that the pizzas be delivered at 6:40, so at 5:40 I was home wondering where the pizza was. I called RT back around 6 and asked what was going on - I was told that the person on the phone hadn't looked at the entire order, so I'd been waiting around for nothing. Everyone was really happy when the doorbell rang at 6:40.

My husband asked the driver if he'd already been tipped. He replied "well, sort of". We looked at the receipt. He received $5 to drive ONE MILE. It's a yes or no question. Sort of? What? Do you need more money for a 2 pizza delivery or are you just trying to trick a grieving family? We THEN saw that it was $98 (yes, NINETY EIGHT US DOLLARS) for the 2 pizzas. I called the manager, insisting there must be some mistake. But I was told by the supervisor on duty that customized pizzas are pretty expensive. I asked if there was anything she could do - these weren't very special pizzas. And their L/XL aren't very big. NOPE. That was it.

The girl in my office meant well by ordering something we'd like, but should have started with a veggie pizza and added toppings, rather than taking off and customizing, etc. Also, she thought she was getting heart-shaped pizza. Her heart was in the right place; and Round Table has no heart. They are just another greedy restaurant chain who lost someone as a customer who had so many fond memories after being a loyal fan for decades.<//Review><pictures>None</pictures>< resp>
None<//resp>

< text>
At first it seems like a luxury apartment but location, location, and location. It's off of a major cross streets on Katella Ave & State College Blvd. Now, I didn't realize until we moved in, so many bums congregate around there. We constantly hear bums screaming outside and beware which side your apartment faces. We got the back side of the apartment where it's a dead end street. And two apartments share garage entrances across from each other. First of all, there are constantly cars parked on the street, mostly Uber/Lyft drivers or shady guys waiting to sneak into the gates garage. The main reason I say waiting to sneak into the garage because we've had our storage unit broken into twice. And not just ours, our neighbors storage units as well. The security on property is useless, they just sit in there car at the front side of the garage and never patrol the premises. Never use their storage units, they are built terribly, it is easy to break into them. And worst part of the backside of the apartment are the amount of dumpsters out there. All the apartments near by and the restaurants puts all their dumpster on that street. So you can see dozen dumpsters 4-5 days a week. Not to mention dumpster trucks are just loud AF. If you want to sleep in on a weekday, forget about it. Our apartment was on the first floor so we got see these beautiful dumpsters right in front of our patio.(see photo) We've asked management and maintenance to put the dumpster away from our patio, where there's plenty of space at the end of the street, but I guess that was too much work for the maintenance crew. Also, they had the fire alarm go off constantly. For what they charge for rent, you can find lot better luxary apartments in the area for the similar costs. I would never go back to this place.< /text>

<Rate>5<//Rate><review>I have been living here a little over a year and overall I love this place. The bathrooms are covered in luxurious travertine tile and the high ceilings in my unit make my place look much bigger than it is. The staff here are friendly and the recent management change is more responsive to tenant requests and also very helpful. Even during this holiday season when things are busy, the leasing office was willing to help with my Christmas package deliveries despite being on their own personal lunch breaks. Alice and Andre are very friendly and residents here seem to socialize a lot with them. Lately there are a lot of events that bring the residents together and they were nicely done.

This community however, is not perfect just like any of the other communities that I have lived in before. I live near the courtyard and the echo can be quite bothersome when residents host their parties in the club room and especially when there's alcohol. Recently, there was an incident around 10 at night when the DJ and guests were being so loud that the management had to step in. There was a lot of yelling and shouting from the drunk guests but in the end I think they were asked to leave. Where's security when you need them? I hope the management will consider banning alcohol because things are getting out of hand lately. Sadly, some people just can't handle their alcohol.

Unsurprisingly, the resident parking garage has a lot of expensive cars and that's to be expected from this demographic who can afford the high rent. However, people here have a tendency to drive pretty fast in the underground garage and I hope they will either install speed bumps and/or post speed limit signs. You see more German marques than other imports and the "spirited" way they are being driven here definitely seems to reflect that.

Overall, the management does a great job despite having to deal with some noisy people partying every now and then. Watch out for the drivers who think the garage is the autobahn.< /review>< Pictures>
